<text>I've been coming here since I was a tiny child. The food is always amazing, the service extraordinary, and everyone is family. Paul frequently has a book to loan my parents, I've often seen customers getting hugs goodbye as they leave, and the smiles on everyone's faces are genuine.

It can be a little loud for date night, but if you don't mind everyone around you heartily enjoying themselves, I'd not hesitate to tell you to bring a first (or second, or seven hundredth) date. Families are always welcome, too, and small children are fond of the penny candy machine near the door. I had my wedding dinner here when my late husband and I eloped, and it was a joy to celebrate my wedding with the restaurant I've grown up with.

Try the house red, anything on the specials list, the Roman Holiday salad, and the gnocchi. Nothing on the menu will disappoint, but those are my favorites.</text><Pics>None</Pics>< response>

Surprisingly good and better than we expected from reading reviews. The meat Cannelloni not only had wonderful thin tender home made crepes wrapping them but also had a red sauce with cream that made it the best I've ever tasted!  Bread had the crispy, crunchy crust it should, the house salad was great, and the Tiramisu was about as good as it gets.  My espresso was accompanied with a couple of home made biscottis which also were terrific. We custom ordered our chicken Picatta with a breaded and fried cutlet, which our super friendly and attentive server Christina accommodated us with cheerfully, and savored the fairly strong lemon caper sauce.  All in all we enjoyed everything about our dinner and felt comfortable and welcomed even as returning home from a day on Stinson Beach.  We definitely recommend this cozy restaurant and can't wait to go back!< /review>

<response>None<//response><Review>I hate to seemingly be the only person on earth who has a negative review to post. My mother and I have been a bit disappointed the past 4 times we ate at Fradelizio's, but kept going back because we love the atmosphere. After a while your memory fades and you forget why you had been disappointed the last time you were there.
It is very cozy and inviting and the staff is always very friendly and accommodating.  My mother ordered the Carbinara. The menu lists this dish as simply 'Carbinara'. No description at all, so when the dish arrived not at all what we excepted, it was a bit of a let down. Carbinara is most commonly made with bacon or panceta, and eggs tossed in. This was instead a creamy mushroom Carbinara, and if there was any bacon in it all, you couldn't tell. Not very tasty.
I ordered the Shrimp Scampi. The menu describes the wine garlic butter sauce...but makes no mention at all about the penne pasta with marinara sauce that is served along side of the shrimp. So there is two major sauces served, together on the same plate, running together. Not good. I had hoped for rice along with the scampi, which is most commonly offered.
Afterwards we ordered each a Cappuccino. Although it is served with a small but very tasty biscotti along side, even this was a disappointment. The Cappuccino was very weak in flavor, and luke warm!  (I remember it being this way last time also.)
For the price we paid, we left feeling very underwhelmed. Love the ambiance, love the friendliness...but I don't think we'll be going back any time soon.</Review>< username>

< text>
I have a new German Shepherd puppy that was in serious need of basic training because of his extremely high energy. I live alone which made the desire to have him under control even more of a necessity. When he was too young to get a rabies shot (14 weeks old) I found a private trainer that would accept him for 3 week basic obedience and keep him separate from any other dogs (full shots are a necessary requirement). That did help some and gave him a decent head start, but the results after a lot of $$ and 3 weeks away from my new puppy were not everything that is advertised, which is generally the same for most puppy ‚Äúboot camps‚Äù. When he was a couple months older with all of his shots and much more work with him on my own at home, I decided to look for a more comprehensive training facility and was recommended K-9 Companions from somebody at the doggie day care he goes to. When I took him in for evaluation I anticipated that he would be going to the intermediate/off leash, 2nd level program. He was way ahead of the game from a first timer but not up to the standards K-9 Companions expects after their 1st level of obedience. He had to brush up and advance his basic training (sit, stay, heel, down, come, no, off...) for one week and was able to move on to the next level for the next 2 weeks. He came back a different dog! Still as sweet and playful as he had been from day 1, but he obeyed everything he was taught as if he was having fun doing it. When I take him for walks or anyone comes to the house, every single person who meets him can‚Äôt believe how well behaved he is for such an energetic puppy. I have even recommended to several people that they take their misbehaving or untrained adult dogs to K-9 Companions for at least basic obedience. I am certain that it has done as much for my dog‚Äôs quality of life as it has for my own enjoyment of him, and believe that would be true for any dog owner/parent. After a couple more months at home with me, he does SO well and enjoys working on everything he has learned so much, I decided to put him through more advanced training. I had already taken him back for short boarding and brush up training and he absolutely loves the staff, as they do him. No separation anxiety at all (I may have a little:) and he was genuinely excited to be back. There was no hesitation at all as the quality of the facility and the care he is given there is top notch. In researching dog training facilities the first thing reviewers and experts say is to do your homework on the facility, they are not all equal. I am 100% comfortable knowing my baby is in great hands at K-9 companions. He is currently there as I‚Äôm writing, going through his off-leash and advanced training. I could not recommend this facility and their staff any more than saying my dog is now on his third stay there and I know he is loving it as much as I will be when he comes home. The follow up training that is included has been invaluable more in the sense of training ME than my dog. He knows exactly what to do, it‚Äôs up to me to know how to properly communicate with positive reinforcement. This training is worth every penny and will pay back dividends with years of enjoyment for both you and your dog. I have owned many dogs throughout my life and never had one formally trained. I thought they were so smart (they were) but had never realized their full potential. I thought my own training that only came from years of repetition was enough. I had no idea the difference professional training would make and am now a firm believer that if anybody has the means to do it, like me they would consider it a necessity.< /text>

117038317758722954521< /UserId.>
<user_name>Laura Gwin</user_name><Time>1457396868030</Time><Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
I think it is important for anyone considering a free consultation at K-9 Companions to understand that the reason for the consultation is to evaluate the dogs temperament and the needs of both the dog and the client. Some dogs need to see a veterinarian for medical or temperament issues due to medical issues prior to training. Some people wish to train their dogs in a manner that is as inexpensive as possible and therefore need to spend more time being involved in the training themselves (such as driving to the facility weekly) and not boarding the dog while training. Other clients prefer to have as much as possible done for them and would prefer to board the dog (costs more) and have as much of the training as possible done for them. Some dogs actually need this level of training due to a lack of socialization or due to them being fearful or aggressive. There is no way that a trainer can tell an owner over the phone what the dog is going to need. This is why the consultation is FREE. The training prescribed could be as little as a (local) in home lesson for $100.00. It could be lessons at the facility for $250-$495. The client might want lessons done in their home (at a higher cost) or they might want the Mercedes of dog training which involves the dog staying (boarding) at the facility, followed by lesson/s in their home and a number of follow up lessons over the next year at the facility.<//Text>

9 days into doggy training (August 11th), I received 4 back to back phone calls from a blocked number. I had my wife call and K9 Companions said Hank wasn't looking well so they took him to the vet. About an hour after they brought him back from the vet, they called saying we needed to pick him up immediately and take him to our vet. When we picked Hank up, he couldn't stand up and could barely lift his head. I had to carry him. You could tell he was extremely ill.

I took him to our local vet and the Dr took one look at Hank and said this is extremely concerning. He did X-rays and ran a parvo test. Hank came back negative for parvo and didn't have any foreign bodies lodged in his stomach but he had fluid in his lungs and was running a high fever. The vet told me, if I do not take Hank to the 24/7 emergency vet in Ontario, that Hank would not make it through the night.

I rushed Hank down the mountain and he was admitted immediately on the spot. The vet told me that Hank was in extremely rough shape and there is a chance he will not see the following morning.

Hank spent 5 days at the emergency vet with 24/7 care. Fortunately, he pulled through. He contracted a viral infection, a bacterial infection, para influenza and developed and pneumonia. Our total medical bills were over $6,000. The vet said he contracted it from this place.

K9 Companion assured us that they have never seen a case like this and that there have been no other cases of dogs getting this sick. The K9 companion staff seemed to be concerned about Hank the entire time, until it was time to talk about the bill. Dianne, the manager, was extremely worried about Hank and genuinely cared about Hanks health. She presented all the findings and bills to the owner. The owner, Laura said, there will be no reimbursement for Hanks medical bills.

K9 Companions is responsible for almost killing my dog and burying me in a financial hole. My wife stays at home with our 16 month old son. I am the sole provider. Our bills are worth two months of pay and we still have to take Hank in to be checked frequently to make sure his lungs have 100% recovered.

Once Hank returned home we had multiple vet visits and required attention at all times from my wife. We had to cancel a family vacation that was planned due to this nightmare. After 4 weeks of being on 3 different types of medication, having to doing breathing treatments, under constant supervision and having to be extremely careful with him, our puppy is starting to act like himself again. Bottom line is, do not take your dog here unless you want to deal with what we have dealt with. Morality has taken a back seat to these people and all they care about are pure profits.

< Review>
Well you have to start off by realizing this is Ridgecrest! It's on us-395 somewhere between nowhere and somewhere. But it is a long way to any other dog parks so it is nice to have this break if you're heading up 395. The park is well fenced there are a lot of big shade trees the only real concern I would warn you about is that it doesn't appear in Ridgecrest that you were required to pick up your dog's poop if it's anywhere near a fence. So the perimeter of the park is lined with biological landmines. But it has grass, and it is in the middle of nowhere. So this part is definitely a 4 or a little above star<//Review>

This was a horrible experience. We have used this company before and gave them 5 stars but will be changing that review on yelp shortly as we feel they probably ripped us off BIG time (shame on us).

We called them out for a noise we were hearing.  They said there was air in the pipes calling it water hammer and suggested we put in new valves behind the washer.  To do this they had to make holes in the wall.  They said it would be $3000. Foolishly we agreed.  The guy worked on it all day and when he went to turn the water back on he forgot to turn off the valves in the laundry room and water shot out into the laundry and kitchen onto the hard wood floors. We had another plumber come and within an hour he had gone under the house, found and fixed the problem and only charged us $140.00.  We have had no problem since.

We feel this company rips you off and charges way too much and their technicians are not well trained.
Run as fast as you can.</Text>
